\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00003}00003\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ rshapes\ -\/\ Basic\ functions\ to\ draw\ 2d\ shapes\ and\ check\ collisions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00004}00004\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00005}00005\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00006}00006\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ Shapes\ can\ be\ draw\ using\ 3\ types\ of\ primitives:\ LINES,\ TRIANGLES\ and\ QUADS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00007}00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ Some\ functions\ implement\ two\ drawing\ options:\ TRIANGLES\ and\ QUADS,\ by\ default\ TRIANGLES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00008}00008\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ are\ used\ but\ QUADS\ implementation\ can\ be\ selected\ with\ SUPPORT\_QUADS\_DRAW\_MODE\ define}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00009}00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00010}00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ Some\ functions\ define\ texture\ coordinates\ (rlTexCoord2f())\ for\ the\ shapes\ and\ use\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00011}00011\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ user-\/provided\ texture\ with\ SetShapesTexture(),\ the\ pourpouse\ of\ this\ implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00012}00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ is\ allowing\ to\ reduce\ draw\ calls\ when\ combined\ with\ a\ texture-\/atlas.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00013}00013\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00014}00014\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ By\ default,\ raylib\ sets\ the\ default\ texture\ and\ rectangle\ at\ InitWindow()[rcore]\ to\ one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00015}00015\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ white\ character\ of\ default\ font\ [rtext],\ this\ way,\ raylib\ text\ and\ shapes\ can\ be\ draw\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rshapes_8c_source_l00016}00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ a\ single\ draw\ call\ and\ it\ also\ allows\ users\ to\ configure\ it\ the\ same\ way\ with\ their\ own\ fonts.}}
